Method: 基于包含非最小引力-物质耦合的修正作用量，推导出修正的爱因斯坦方程，并分析不同高能动力学下（尤其是牛顿常数趋于零）引力坍缩所形成的时空几何结构。

Result: 发现了三类无奇点的渐近核心结构：德西特、闵可夫斯基和‘陡压’型；其中，只有当牛顿常数在趋于零前变为负值时，才会出现闵可夫斯基核心。这一特性与非最小耦合的具体形式及流体状态方程无关。

Conclusion: 牛顿常数在高能极限下变为负值是形成闵可夫斯基核心的必要条件，该结果具有普适性，不依赖于具体模型细节。

Abstract: Modified Einstein's equations implementing both an energy-dependent Newtonian
and cosmological constant can be obtained via a modified action characterised
by a non-minimal gravity-matter coupling. We show how different dynamics for
the high energy regime - that nevertheless have in common the vanishing of the
Newton constant - result in models of gravitational collapse which source the
formation of non-singular geometries with different types of asymptotic core:
de Sitter, Minkowski, and with "steep pressure". As we categorise their
defining properties, one feature, which we prove to be actually independent of

### [112] [Black-hole ringdown analysis with inspiral-merger informed templates and limitations of classical spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.17315)
*Koustav Chandra,Juan Calderón Bustillo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于完整引力波波形模型的黑洞并合后环down分析方法，通过结合二元系统参数自然包含所有准正规模（QNMs），避免了传统半无知谱分析中的多余自由度和不一致先验问题。对GW150914的分析显示对无毛定理的强证据（贝叶斯因子>650:1），并验证了该方法在模拟信号中准确恢复残余黑洞性质的能力。研究还表明，仅依赖泛音检测的经典谱分析难以实现强有力的无毛检验，且由于QNMs的非正交性，模式解释具有模型依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统半无知环down分析忽略并合起源，导致自由参数过多和先验不一致，难以有效检验广义相对论预测的黑洞无毛定理。因此需要一种更物理一致的方法来充分利用引力波数据。

Method: 采用完整的IMR波形模型（NRSur7dq4）的并合后部分进行环down建模，自然包含所有准正规模，并将先验与二元系统参数关联。使用贝叶斯推断分析真实和模拟信号，评估不同模型对无毛定理检验的能力。

Result: 对GW150914分析得到>650:1的贝叶斯因子支持无毛定理，远高于传统方法的3:1；发现约5:1的证据支持(2,2,1)泛音，无更高模式证据；模拟验证了残余性质的准确恢复；证明经典谱分析受限于信噪比和模式非正交性，难以提供强检验。

Conclusion: 基于IMR模型的环down分析能更有效地检验无毛定理，减少人为假设，提高物理一致性。未来高信噪比事件需考虑模式非正交性和模型依赖性，以避免误导性解释。

Abstract: The ringdown of a perturbed black hole consists of a superposition of
quasi-normal modes (QNMs), with complex frequencies determined by the black
hole's mass and spin, while phases and amplitudes depend on binary parameters.
Traditional semi-agnostic ringdown analyses ignore the remnant's binary-merger
origin, assuming instead generic perturbations. This can lead to an unphysical
number of free parameters and usage of priors inconsistent with those imposed
by full inspiral-merger-ringdown (IMR) analysis. Here we revisit an alternative
approach, first proposed in Calder\'on Bustillo et al. 2021, in which ringdowns
are modeled using the post-merger portion of full IMR waveform models. This
naturally includes all QNMs without adding extra degrees of freedom and ties
priors to binary parameters. We analyze the signal GW150914 with the
post-merger portion of the IMR surrogate model NRSur7dq4, finding decisive
evidence for the no-hair theorem with a Bayes factor $>650:1$ or $>99.8$%
probability, compared to only $3:1$ from semi-agnostic spectroscopy, consistent
with previous work. We also find modest evidence ($\simeq 5:1$) for the
$(\ell,m,n)=(2,2,1)$ overtone and none for higher modes. Using simulated
signals, we validate our formalism by showing accurate recovery of remnant
properties. Next, by analysing simulated signals with post-merger
signal-to-noise ratios up to 100, we show that classical spectroscopy based on
overtone detection alone cannot provide strong no-hair tests. Finally, we
demonstrate that the non-orthogonality of QNMs makes the inferred mode content
strongly model-dependent, leading to multiple inconsistent interpretations that
are equally well-supported by the data. We briefly discuss potential
implications for recent events, such as GW231123 and GW250114.

</details>

Abstract: We test the weak cosmic censorship conjecture (WCCC) for the

component is significant during radiation-dominated epochs, and becomes
naturally negligible as the universe transitions to the matter-dominated era.

### [115] [Exact Taub-NUT-like Black Holes in Einstein-bumblebee gravity: their thermodynamics and thermodynamic topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.17407)

### [120] [Observational constraints on the nonlinear regime of gravity with a parametrized beyond-GR gravitational waveform model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.17592)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Watarai等人（2024）提出的修正波形模型，对GW150914事件进行参数化分析，提取并合阶段可能偏离广义相对论的参数，并将其转化为对物理量（如额外辐射能量和并合时间偏差）的模型无关约束。

Result: 对于GW150914，并合阶段额外辐射的能量被限制为广义相对论预测总能量的$0.26^{+0.75}_{-0.62}\%$，并合时间偏差为$2.17^{+9.56}_{-9.90}~\mathrm{ms}$（90%置信区间）。

Abstract: Gravitational waves from compact binary coalescences provide unique
opportunities to test general relativity (GR) in the strong-field regime. In
particular, the merger phase, during which two compact objects finally
coalesce, corresponds to the regime of the strongest gravitational fields
accessible by direct observation and thus serves as a probe of the nonlinear
nature of gravity. In this work, we test GR in the merger phase by analyzing
GW150914 using a modified waveform proposed in [Watarai et al. 2024], which
parametrizes possible deviations from GR during this stage. Within this
framework, the inferred deviation parameters can be translated into
model-independent constraints on physically meaningful quantities. For
GW150914, we find that the additional energy radiated in the merger phase is
constrained to be $0.26^{+0.75}_{-0.62}~\%$ of the total energy emitted over
the entire coalescence predicted by GR, and the deviation in the coalescence
time is $2.17^{+9.56}_{-9.90}~\mathrm{ms}$, both within the $90\%$ credible
interval. These two constraints serve as observational benchmarks for
deviations in the nonlinear gravity regime, offering guidance for theoretical
investigations of beyond-GR models.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现相同类型的粒子（玻色子或费米子）在相同量子数l下具有相同的准束缚频率，但不同类型粒子之间频率永不相等。

Conclusion: 电磁波在特定条件下可以用来模拟引力波行为，为未来实验提供了理论基础和可检验预测。

Abstract: We show that, in Schwarzschild equivalent mediums, the massless spin
particles obey the same dynamical equation, from which we obtain remarkably
simple formulae for the frequencies of the quasibound states. We find that the
quasibound frequencies of different bosons can be identical at the same quantum
number $l$, and the same is true of different fermions, but a quasibound
frequency for bosons can never equal a quasibound frequency for fermions. These
results mean that, in Schwarzschild equivalent mediums with the
quasibound-state boundary conditions, characteristics of electromagnetic waves
are the same as those for all the massless bosonic waves, thereby allowing
electromagnetic waves to simulate gravitational waves. Our predictions can be
tested in future experiments, building upon the successful preparation of
Schwarzschild equivalent mediums.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过构造满足特定物理边界条件的单调熵泛函，将洛伦兹时空的里奇流与密度函数的共轭热流耦合，作为熵泛函在约束下的梯度流，利用泛函的有界性控制整体系统的演化。

Abstract: This paper attempts to construct monotonic entropy functionals for

conditions, as an extension of Perelman's monotonic entropy functionals
constructed for three-dimensional compact Riemannian manifolds. The
monotonicity of these entropy functionals is utilized to prove the
well-posedness of applying Ricci flow to four-dimensional Lorentzian spacetime,
particularly for the timelike modes which would seem blow up and ill-defined.
The general idea is that the the Ricci flow of a Lorentzian spacetime metric
and the coupled conjugate heat flow of a density on the Lorentzian spacetime as
a whole turns out to be the gradient flows of the monotonic functionals under
some imposed constraint, so the superficial "blow-up" in the individual Ricci
flow system or the conjugate heat flow system contradicts the boundedness of
the monotonic functionals within finite flow interval, which gives a global
control to the whole coupled system. The physical significance and applications
of these monotonic entropy functionals in real gravitational systems are also
discussed.

critical orbits, and determining the resulting black hole shadow. To complement
these analyses, we explore gravitational lensing by evaluating the deflection
angle in both the weak- and strong-field regimes. Using these results,
constraints are derived for the lensing observables by comparing with the Event
Horizon Telescope data for $Sgr A^{*}$ and $M87^{*}$. Finally, we close the
analysis by deriving additional constraints from standard Solar System
experiments, including Mercury's orbital precession, gravitational light
bending, and time-delay measurements.

</details>


### [126] [Non-linearly scalarized supermassive black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.17892)
*Shoupan Liu,Yunqi Liu,Yan Peng,Cheng-Yong Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究了在包含平方高斯-博内项的标量-高斯-博内引力框架中，非线性机制如何驱动旋转黑洞的标量化形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在修正引力理论中，Kerr黑洞在线性稳定但非线性不稳定的条件下如何发生标量化。

Method: 采用伪谱方法求解非线性标量化的旋转黑洞解谱，并分析其热力学性质。

Result: 发现了多个标量化分支，表明黑洞自旋和额外的平方高斯-博内项显著影响解的存在性和性质；标量化黑洞在相同质量和自旋下比Kerr黑洞具有更高的熵。

Conclusion: 非线性标量化在修正引力中起关键作用，且标量化黑洞在热力学上更优。

Abstract: In this study, we investigate a nonlinear mechanism driving the formation of
scalarized rotating black holes within a scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity framework
that includes an additional squared Gauss-Bonnet term. With the specific
coupling function, Kerr metric is a solution to this modified gravity. In
linear level Kerr black holes are stable against the scalar perturbation, while
nonlinearly they suffer the so-called ``nonlinear scalarization" and are
unstable. By employing a pseudo-spectral method, we derive the spectrum of
nonlinearly scalarized rotating black hole solutions, revealing multiple
scalarized branches. Our analysis demonstrates that both the black hole's spin
and the additional squared Gauss-Bonnet term significantly influence the
existence and properties of these solutions. Furthermore, we explore the
thermodynamic properties of nonlinearly scalarized rotating black holes, and
find that the scalarized black holes are entropically favored over Kerr black
holes of the same mass and spin across a wide range of parameters.

</details>


### [127] [Global stability of ghostly field theories: Classical scattering in $(N+1)$ dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.18049)
*Aaron Held*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文回顾了小数据全局稳定性的结果，并探讨其在具有相反符号动能项（幽灵）的经典相互作用标量场中的应用。通过球对称假设下的数值散射解，发现某些具有多项式相互作用势的幽灵场理论在所有紧支撑初始条件下也表现出全局稳定性，表明自相互作用可能抑制幽灵不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究幽灵场的不稳定性问题，探索是否存在物理机制可以在经典层面上抑制这种不稳定性。

Method: 回顾小数据全局稳定性的理论结果，并基于球对称假设构造一参数族的数值散射解，分析不同多项式相互作用势下的全局稳定性行为。

Result: 识别出一类具有多项式相互作用势的幽灵场理论，在小数据和大数据情况下均表现出全局稳定性，表明强自相互作用可能主导并抑制幽灵不稳定性。

Conclusion: 至少在经典物理框架下，足够强的自相互作用可能提供一种机制来完全抑制幽灵场的不稳定性，从而使得这类理论可能是稳定的且可长期演化的。

Abstract: We review results on small-data global stability and highlight their
applicability to classical interacting scalar fields with opposite-sign kinetic
terms (ghosts). Further, we present a one-parameter family of numerical
scattering solutions under the simplifying assumption of spherical symmetry. We
thereby identify classical ghostly field theories with polynomial interaction
potentials for which small-data global stability apparently extends to
large-data global stability, i.e., global stability for all compactly supported
initial data. These global stability results support an underlying physical
mechanism by which the ghost instability can be quenched due to dominant
self-interactions, at least in classical physics.

</details>


### [128] [Arbitrarily long-lived quasinormal modes of proper-time flow black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.18061)
*Milena Skvortsova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究了渐近安全引力中正则黑洞背景下大质量标量场的准正常模式（QNMs），利用WKB近似和时域积分方法计算了不同参数下的复频率，发现实部随场质量增加，虚部显示长寿命模式特征，且渐近衰减表现为振荡缓慢衰减并带有幂律包络。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在渐近安全引力框架下量子修正黑洞中大质量标量场的准正常模式行为，理解其与经典黑洞（如Schwarzschild）的区别及潜在物理意义。

Method: 采用WKB近似结合Padé重求和以及时域积分方法，计算不同标量场质量μ、角动量数ℓ和变形参数q下的准正常模式复频率。

Result: 准正常模式的实部随标量场质量增大而增加；虚部表现出支持长寿命模式的行为；尽管未观测到准共振，但时域分析显示晚期以振荡性缓慢衰减为主，并具有幂律包络的渐近衰减行为。

Conclusion: 该量子修正黑洞模型中的标量扰动表现出独特的动力学特性，区别于经典黑洞，暗示了量子引力效应对黑洞稳定性和辐射演化的可能影响。

Abstract: We investigate the quasinormal modes (QNMs) of a massive scalar field in the
background of a regular black hole arising from the proper-time flow in
asymptotically safe gravity. This quantum-corrected geometry, characterized by
a deformation parameter q, smoothly interpolates between a near-extremal
regular black hole and the Schwarzschild solution. Employing both the WKB
approximation with Pad\'e resummation and time-domain integration, we compute
the complex frequencies for various values of the scalar field mass $\mu$,
multipole number $\ell$, and deformation parameter q. We observe that the real
parts of the QNMs increase with the field mass, while the imaginary parts
exhibit behavior indicative of long-lived modes. Although quasi-resonances are
not detected in the time-domain profiles due to the dominance of late-time
tails, we find that the asymptotic decay follows an oscillatory slowly decaying
behavior with the power-law envelope.

</details>
